	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/vendor_update.sh');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') != 'f4a529fd7e8aeb0232d98462cc18e10c521de21d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/vendor_update.sh', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/vendor_update.sh');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== 'f4a529fd7e8aeb0232d98462cc18e10c521de21d') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== 'c9e7d6eefe6b2efc99a32acbe425f1dcb5d40582') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/vendor_update.sh')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/vendor_update.sh', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== 'f4a529fd7e8aeb0232d98462cc18e10c521de21d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	writefile_21();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') != '11018885c71809942b078ef83509ff2421fbfcad') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '11018885c71809942b078ef83509ff2421fbfcad') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'e18c3fdee0b2fe2b0836b7333849a7e167ea154f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_21();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '11018885c71809942b078ef83509ff2421fbfcad') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '89ef40b64f15dd39ba6d616f74960c95d8fc82c8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '89ef40b64f15dd39ba6d616f74960c95d8fc82c8') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '68cc2de5ec04544bc5d623df2a84303d5dae6306') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '89ef40b64f15dd39ba6d616f74960c95d8fc82c8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	writefile_26();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') != '0263c2e631820c6233272f3683bda60e82600edd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '0263c2e631820c6233272f3683bda60e82600edd') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '7618cffeb1dbc431b3536426f82ee7991ed20fdf') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '0263c2e631820c6233272f3683bda60e82600edd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_27();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'bcc8ecbe76085b7f846dcc879dc11f712cd02107') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'bcc8ecbe76085b7f846dcc879dc11f712cd02107') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '47ebd7ac6d15fdb1ed30e39746e0f5bc5ee8688b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_27();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'bcc8ecbe76085b7f846dcc879dc11f712cd02107') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_28();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != 'd3ae425af3f27b5fa4613d8121efb8d85f15f73c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'd3ae425af3f27b5fa4613d8121efb8d85f15f73c') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '1581f3bc0c764b262fd31c702e6b79e78ba0ddad') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_28();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'd3ae425af3f27b5fa4613d8121efb8d85f15f73c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
